Welcome to the object database for Super Mario Galaxy and Super Mario Galaxy 2. Here, you can find information about every object and class that can be used in the game. This page lists all objects in the Galaxy games. A brief description and a name should help you get an idea about what an object is used for.

 CrystalSwitchCrystalSwitchCrystal Switch

A Zelda-like crystal switch that can be activated using Spin Attacks, Ground-Pounds, Star Bit
Shots or by trampling on it. This will trigger the event attached to its SW_A setting permanently.
However, if you specify the activation time, it will deactivate again after the set amount of
frames have passed.

By Someone, Evanbowl and Aurum
Our first real custom object with code!

SMG1MapMapPartsInfo
 KoopaJrSmallShipAGuidePointSimpleMapObjAirship Platform Path Marker

A straight line of orange-ish dots that serve as a visual marker of the path the airship platform* takes on Bowser Jr.'s Airship Armada.

Extra notes:
1) This is entirely decoration, the airship platform* can still function perfectly fine without this object.
2) This object not dynamic, meaning you can change the real path taken by the airship platform*, by adding turns for example, and this object will still be a straight line, therefore entirely useless if you change anything on the real path, unless you remodel this object yourself.

* Reference to the KoopaJrSmallShipA object.

BothMapObjInfo
 SpaceCocoonSpaceCocoonSling Pod

A weird spiderweb-like object which Mario and certain NPCs (Toads) can attach to and then be launched in a straight line by pulling it with the star pointer holding A in the opposite direction of the desired launch and then releasing A. How far back you pull it also affects the speed and distance of the launch. There is no way to detach yourself or an NPC to it other than launching.

Extra Notes: If you are setting up a Tarantox battle, do not use this object, but it's special variant for Tarantox called SpiderAttachPoint.
